addHook()

addHook(string  $tag, string|array|callable  $callback, integer  $priority = 10)

Hooks a function onto a specific tag.

Parameters

string $tag

The name of hook.
string|array|callable $callback

The function or class to be called.
integer $priority

Priority that function will be executed. Lower number will be execute earlier. Default is 10.

Throws

\InvalidArgumentException

Throw the exception if argument is wrong type or wrong value.

hasHook()

hasHook(string  $tag, string|array|callable  $callback = false) : boolean|integer

Check if any hook has been registered.

Parameters

string $tag

The name of hook.
string|array|callable $callback

The function or class callback to check for. Default is false.

Throws

\InvalidArgumentException

Throw the exception if argument is wrong type or wrong value.

Returns

boolean|integer —

Return boolean if $callback is set to false. If $callback is check for specific function, the priority of that hook is returned, or return false if not found.

\Rdb\Modules\RdbAdmin\Libraries\Plugins
